## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1224">정규식</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1224">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1225">ASP.NET Core 프레임워크는 정규식 생성자에 `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant`를 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1225">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1226">이러한 멤버에 대한 설명은 <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1226">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1227">정규식은 라우팅 및 C# 언어에서 사용하는 것과 유사한 구분 기호 및 토큰을 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1227">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1228">정규식 토큰은 이스케이프되어야 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1228">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1229">라우팅에서 `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$`라는 정규식을 사용하려면, C# 소스 파일에서는 `\` 문자열 이스케이프 문자를 이스케이프하기 위해서 식 문자열의 `\`(단일 백슬래시) 문자를 `\\`(이중 백슬래시) 문자로 제공해야 합니다([약어 문자열 리터럴](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)을 사용하지 않는 한).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1229">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1230">라우팅 매개 변수 구분 기호 문자(`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`)를 이스케이프하려면 식에서 해당 문자를 이중으로 사용합니다(`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1230">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1231">다음 표는 정규식 및 이스케이프된 버전을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1231">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1232">정규식</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1232">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1233">이스케이프된 정규식</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1233">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1234">라우팅에 사용되는 정규식은 캐럿(`^`) 문자로 시작하고 문자열의 시작 위치와 일치하는 경우가 많습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1234">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1235">식은 달러 기호(`$`) 문자로 끝나고 문자열의 끝과 일치하는 경우가 많습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1235">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1236">`^` 및 `$` 문자는 정규식이 전체 경로 매개 변수 값과 일치하도록 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1236">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1237">`^` 및 `$` 문자가 없는 정규식은 문자열 내의 모든 하위 문자열과 일치하는데, 이는 종종 원하는 것이 아닙니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1237">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1238">다음 표에서는 예제를 제공하고, 일치하거나 일치에 실패하는 이유를 설명합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1238">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1239">식</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1239">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1240">문자열</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1240">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1241">일치</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1241">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1242">주석</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1242">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1243">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1243">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1244">예</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1244">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1245">부분 문자열 일치</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1245">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1246">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1246">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1247">예</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1247">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1248">부분 문자열 일치</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1248">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1249">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1249">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1250">예</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1250">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1251">식 일치</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1251">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1252">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1252">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1253">예</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1253">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1254">대/소문자 구분하지 않음</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1254">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1255">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1255">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1256">아니요</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1256">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1257">위의 `^` 및 `$` 참조</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1257">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1258">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1258">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1259">아니요</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1259">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1260">위의 `^` 및 `$` 참조</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1260">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1261">정규식 구문에 대한 자세한 내용은 [.NET Framework 정규식](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1261">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1262">가능한 값의 알려진 집합으로 매개 변수를 제한하려면 정규식을 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1262">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1263">예를 들어 `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}`는 `action` 경로 값을 `list`, `get` 또는 `create`으로만 일치시킵니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1263">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1264">제약 조건 사전으로 전달되면 `^(list|get|create)$` 문자열은 동일합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1264">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1265">알려진 제약 조건 중 하나와 일치하지 않는 제약 조건 사전(템플릿 내 인라인이 아님)에서 전달되는 제약 조건도 정규식으로 처리됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1265">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1266">사용자 지정 경로 제약 조건</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1266">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1267">기본 제공 경로 제약 조건 외에도 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 인터페이스를 구현하여 사용자 지정 경로 제약 조건을 만들 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1267">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1268"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 인터페이스에는 제약 조건이 충족되는 경우 `true`를 반환하고 그렇지 않은 경우 `false`를 반환하는 `Match` 단일 메서드가 포함됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1268">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1269">사용자 지정 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>를 사용하려면 앱의 서비스 컨테이너에 있는 앱의 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>에 경로 제약 조건 형식을 등록해야 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1269">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1270"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>은 경로 제약 조건 키를 해당 제약 조건의 유효성을 검사하는 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 구현과 매핑하는 사전입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1270">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1271">`Startup.ConfigureServices`에서 [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) 호출의 일부로 또는 `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`를 사용하여 직접 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions>를 구성하여 앱의 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>을 수정할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1271">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1272">예:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1272">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1273">이제 제약 조건 형식을 등록할 때 지정한 이름을 사용하여 일반적인 방식으로 제약 조건을 경로에 적용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1273">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1274">예:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1274">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1275">URL 생성 참조</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1275">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1276">다음 예제에서는 경로 값의 사전 및 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>이 지정된 경로에 대한 링크를 생성하는 방법을 보여줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1276">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1277">위의 샘플 끝부분에서 생성된 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath>는 `/package/create/123`입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1277">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1278">사전은 "Track Package Route" 템플릿인 `package/{operation}/{id}`의 `operation` 및 `id` 경로 값을 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1278">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1279">자세한 내용은 [라우팅 미들웨어 사용](#use-routing-middleware) 섹션의 샘플 코드 또는 [샘플 앱](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1279">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> 생성자에 대한 두 번째 매개 변수는 *앰비언트 값*의 컬렉션입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1280">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1281">개발자가 요청 컨텍스트 내에서 지정해야 하는 값의 수를 제한하므로 앰비언트 값은 사용하기 편리합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1281">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1282">현재 요청의 현재 경로 값은 링크 생성에 대한 앰비언트 값으로 간주됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1282">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1283">ASP.NET Core MVC 앱의 `HomeController`에 대한 `About` 작업에서는 `Index` 작업에 연결하기 위해 컨트롤러 경로 값을 지정할 필요가 없으며, `Home`이라는 앰비언트 값이 사용됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1283">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1284">매개 변수와 일치하지 않는 앰비언트 값은 무시됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1284">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1285">명시적으로 제공된 값이 앰비언트 값을 재정의하는 경우에도 앰비언트 값이 무시됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1285">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1286">URL에서 일치는 왼쪽에서 오른쪽으로 수행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1286">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1287">명시적으로 제공되지만 경로의 세그먼트와 일치하지 않는 값은 쿼리 문자열에 추가됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1287">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1288">다음 표에서 경로 템플릿 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`를 사용하는 경우 결과를 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1288">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1289">앰비언트 값</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1289">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1290">명시적 값</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1290">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1291">결과</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1291">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1292">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1292">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1293">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1293">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1294">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1294">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1295">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1295">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1296">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1296">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1297">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1297">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1298">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1298">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1299">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1299">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1300">경로에 매개 변수에 해당하지 않고 값이 명시적으로 제공된 기본값이 있는 경우 기본값과 일치해야 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1300">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1301">`controller` 및 `action`에 대해 일치하는 값이 제공되는 경우에만 링크 생성에서 이 경로에 대한 링크를 생성합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1301">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1302">복잡한 세그먼트</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1302">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1303">복잡한 세그먼트(예: `[Route("/x{token}y")]`)는 non-greedy 방식으로 오른쪽에서 왼쪽으로 리터럴을 매칭하여 처리됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1303">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1304">복잡한 세그먼트 일치 방법에 대한 자세한 설명은 [이 코드](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1304">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dff3f-1305">[코드 샘플](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)은 ASP.NET Core에서 사용되지 않지만 복잡한 세그먼트에 대한 적절한 설명을 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dff3f-1305">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
<!-- While that code is no longer used by ASP.NET Core for complex segment matching, it provides a good match to the current algorithm. The [current code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/91514c9af7e0f4c44029b51f05a01c6fe4c96e4c/src/Http/Routing/src/Matching/DfaMatcherBuilder.cs#L227-L244) is too abstracted from matching to be useful for understanding complex segment matching.
